<span id="freeTextContainer1434556010872056545">It is done. I read it. I am so exhausted. Hallowed really did something to me. I had butterflies in my stomach,I was happy when Tucker showed up(duh),I was annoyed with the stupidity of the secondary characters,angry at Clara for not giving her relationship with Tucker a real chance. Bawled my eyes out over that heartbreaking ending. <br/><br/><br/><blockquote>You see these pictures? What is wrong with them? (Aside from the fact Clara is a giant and poor Tucker is too small. I had no idea I cropped and re-sized his photo </blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText1434556010872056545" style="display:none">It is done. I read it. I am so exhausted. Hallowed really did something to me. I had butterflies in my stomach,I was happy when Tucker showed up(duh),I was annoyed with the stupidity of the secondary characters,angry at Clara for not giving her relationship with Tucker a real chance. Bawled my eyes out over that heartbreaking ending. <br><br><br><blockquote>You see these pictures? What is wrong with them? (Aside from the fact Clara is a giant and poor Tucker is too small. I had no idea I cropped and re-sized his photo that much. Sorry Tuck.)</blockquote><br><a href="http://s1117.photobucket.com/albums/k588/Zemmy-hearts-books/?action=view&amp;current=tuckeredited.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380345806i/700400.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://s1117.photobucket.com/albums/k588/Zemmy-hearts-books/?action=view&amp;current=claraedited.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380345806i/700401.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://s1117.photobucket.com/albums/k588/Zemmy-hearts-books/?action=view&amp;current=christianedited.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380345806i/700402.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><blockquote>I'll tell you what! Christian is there. Dude you need to disappear or Tucker fangirls will get you.</blockquote><br><br><br>You know,sometimes a love triangle works. But right now I can't think of any book like that. :/ Here we have Tucker,a sweet and irresistible cowboy and Christian,the 'perfect guy'. Now,Tucker already has the girl but I felt like Clara's relationship with him is totally different in this book than it was in the first one. Here she is hiding things from Tucker and they obviously got over that Honeymoon stage. Christian on the other hand is acting like a guardian angel. Even even though we learn more about his past and his character that wasn't enough for me to like him. He is still a typical YA guy. Often in these love triangles you can obviously guess which two are made for each other. I got really confused because I really though Tucker was THE GUY for Clara. Now I'm just saving money for a plane ticket to Wyoming so I can get some sweet Tucker action. <i>Baby I wan be your rebound girl.</i> *wink* Ugh,this sounds so nasty.<br><br>Now to the secondary characters rant. Yeffrey. You remember him? The funny younger brother? He is gone. Say hello to Yeffrey-lame ass punk who talks back to his family and friends. The one who gets sick of standing in Clara's shadow. Well I can't really blame him for the second part but you have to believe me when I say he was really awful. <br><br>Angela was this mysterious girl who I though was kinda cool but now she snaps at Clara for keeping stuff from her while she is the one that writes in her diary and doesn't let anyone near it. I still think she will be evil in upcoming books. <br><br>Wendy never truly appealed to me but I was on her side in the first book when she pushed Clara to like Tucker and not the Perfect Guy. In this book I wanted to smash her face a few times for the reasons I can't really remember. What was she like? Obnoxious most of the time. She was so judgy. <br><br>Clara's mother and her secrets are the best part of the book. I wanted to know what her purpose was and I wan't disappointed with the ending. Cynthia sure knows how to keep my attention because it never got to the boring part. Also we get to see a certain someone who is important to Clara and Yeffrey. Get ready for a surprise you two because he has some important things to say to you. <br><br><br>Not sure how will I rate Hallowed. Many things annoyed the heck out of me. But I did cry which is my indicator the book obviously did something good. And I still look forward to the day when I get my book delivered.<br><br><br>Don't be too harsh on me guys. I know this review sucks. </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('AD9uCqiBFdY2+sCje1u3q0L1xH25kOKJ7X9NpVhP5HMc0pwxpAwkub9s9CNMcV5CEk2+Vn1eu5y8MCqxY6ckww==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('cmz/6DylzDjnFlMvQrAKoOdizw4CBj1h023rAOjRSVlugQ3TMCj9V26AZ691muNJt9q1JcbIZHSCIowU0zmJ6Q==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer7403832755298163658">Cynthia Hand is the New York Times bestselling author of several books for teens, including the UNEARTHLY trilogy, THE LAST TIME WE SAY GOODBYE, MY LADY JANE and MY PLAIN JANE (with fellow authors Brodi Ashton and Jodi Meadows), THE AFTERLIFE OF HOLLY CHASE, and the upcoming novels THE HOW AND THE WHY and MY CALAMITY JANE (also with Ashton and Meadows). Before turning to writing for young adults, </span>
  <span id="freeText7403832755298163658" style="display:none">Cynthia Hand is the New York Times bestselling author of several books for teens, including the UNEARTHLY trilogy, THE LAST TIME WE SAY GOODBYE, MY LADY JANE and MY PLAIN JANE (with fellow authors Brodi Ashton and Jodi Meadows), THE AFTERLIFE OF HOLLY CHASE, and the upcoming novels THE HOW AND THE WHY and MY CALAMITY JANE (also with Ashton and Meadows). Before turning to writing for young adults, she studied literary fiction and earned both an M.F.A. and a Ph.D. in fiction writing. She currently resides in Boise, Idaho, with her husband, two cats, one crazy dog, two kids, and mountain of books.</span>
